  <script>_satellite["_runScript1"](function(event, target, Promise) {

/**

 * @returns string category or product code by URL

 */

const getCategory = () => {

  var splitedURL = window.location.href.split("/");



  if (getPageType() == "PLP") {

    if (splitedURL.indexOf("category") != -1) {

      return splitedURL[splitedURL.indexOf("category") + 1].trim();

    } else if (splitedURL.indexOf("collection") != -1) {

      return (

        splitedURL[splitedURL.indexOf("collection") + 1].trim().split("?")[0] ||

        "none"

      );

    }

    return null;

  } else if (getPageType() == "PDP") {

    if (splitedURL.indexOf("product") != -1) {

      return splitedURL[splitedURL.indexOf("product") + 1].trim();

    }

  } else if (getPageType() == "SLP") {

    return "S";

  } else if (getPageType() == "Page") {

    if (splitedURL.indexOf("page") != -1) {

      return (

        splitedURL[splitedURL.indexOf("page") + 1].trim().split("?")[0] ||

        "none"

      );

    }

  }

  return "none";

};



/**

 *

 * @param parameterName string name of parameter to search

 * @returns parameter value if found or else null

 */

const getParameter = (parameterName) => {

  var params = window.location.search;

  params = params.replace("?", "").split("&");



  params = params.filter(function (p) {

    return p.includes(parameterName + "=");

  });



  return params.length > 0 ? params[0].split("=")[1] : null;

};



/**

 *

 * @returns string page type by URL

 */

const getPageType = () => {

  if (

    /category/i.test(window.location.href) ||

    /collection/i.test(window.location.href)

  ) {

    return "PLP";

  }



  if (/search/i.test(window.location.href)) {

    return "SLP";

  }



  if (/product/i.test(window.location.href)) {

    return "PDP";

  }



  if (/page/i.test(window.location.href)) {

    return "Page";

  }



  return "Home";

};



const createDigitalData = () => {

  if (typeof window.digitalData === "undefined") {

    window.digitalData = {};

  }



  if (window.digitalData) {

    if (typeof window.digitalData.storage === "undefined") {

      window.digitalData.storage = {};

      return true;

    } else {

      return true;

    }

  }

  return false;

};



const setCookie = (cname, cvalue, exdays) => {

  var d = new Date();

  d.setTime(d.getTime() + exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);

  var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();

  document.cookie =

    cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/;domain=.falabella.com";

};



/**

 *

 * Get cookie

 *

 * @param {String} cname Cookie Name

 * @returns {String} Cookie value

 */

const getCookie = (cname) => {

  var name = cname + "=";

  var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);

  var ca = decodedCookie.split(";");

  for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {

    var c = ca[i];

    while (c.charAt(0) == " ") {

      c = c.substring(1);

    }

    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {

      return c.substring(name.length, c.length);

    }

  }

  return null;

};

  <script>_satellite["_runScript3"](function(event, target, Promise) {

/*************************************************************************************************************

*	Adobe Consulting Plugin: getPercentPageViewed v6.0.0

*

*	Release Date: 2021-07-26

* 

*	Arguments to Pass In:

*	@param {String} pid a variable that you want to tie the percentage of page viewed to.  This would usually be some sort of page identifier.  Defaults to the Analytics pageName OR the current URL if not set.

*	@param {Boolean} change set this equal to false if you don't want the plugin to take into consideration any changes made to the page size after its initial load.  true is the recommended/default value for this argument

*			

*	@returns {Object} 

*		An object with the following variables:

*			ppvPreviousPage = The name of the previous page viewed (Since final measurements aren't available until a NEW page loads) 

*			ppvHighestPercentViewed = The highest percent of the previous page that the visitor viewed (height-wise); in other words, what was the furthest point that the visitor scrolled down on the page

*			ppvInitialPercentViewed = The percent of the previous page that was visible when the previous page *first* loaded

*			ppvHighestPixelsSeen = The highest number of total pixels seen (height-wise) as the visitor scrolled down the previous page

*			ppvFoldsSeen = The highest number of total "page folds" seen as the visitor scrolled down the previous page (including the "top-of-page" fold)

*			ppvFoldsAvailable = The number of total "page folds" available to scroll down on the previous page 

*

*

*************************************************************************************************************/

function getPercentPageViewed(pid, change)

{

	if(pid === "-v") return {"plugin": "getPercentPageViewed", "version": "6.0.0"}

	window.cookieRead=window.cookieRead||function(k){if("string"===typeof k)k=encodeURIComponent(k);else return"";var c=" "+document.cookie,b=c.indexOf(" "+k+"="),d=0>b?b:c.indexOf(";",b);return(k=0>b?"":decodeURIComponent(c.substring(b+2+k.length,0>d?c.length:d)))?k:""};

	function handlePPVevents()

	{

		//return nothing if ppvID hasn't been set yet. 

		if(!window.ppvID) return;



		var getValue = function( name ) {

			var r;

			try { r = Math.max( document.body[name], document.documentElement[name] ) } 

			catch(e) { 

				try { r = document.body[name] }

				catch(e) {

					try { r = document.documentElement[name] }

					catch(e) { r = 0 }

				}

			}

			return r;

		},

		//set documentHeight equal to the height (in pixels) of the entire web page

		documentHeight = Math.max( getValue( 'scrollHeight' ), getValue( 'offsetHeight' ), getValue( 'clientHeight' ) ),



		//set browserWindowHeight equal to the height (in pixels) of the browser window's visible portion

		browserWindowHeight = window.innerHeight || getValue( 'clientHeight' ),



		//set pixelsDown equal to the number of pixels that the visitor has scrolled down from the top of the page

		pixelsDown = window.pageYOffset || getValue( 'scrollTop' ),



		//set totalPixelsSeen equal to how many pixels (height-wise) that the visitor has seen of the page

		totalPixelsSeen = pixelsDown + browserWindowHeight,



		//set percentPixelsViewed equal to the % of pixels (height-wise that the visitor has seen of the page

		percentPixelsViewed = Math.min( Math.round( totalPixelsSeen / documentHeight * 100 ), 100 ),



		//set foldsSeen equal to the number of below-the-folds equivalent seen (including the top-of-page fold)

		foldsSeen = Math.floor( totalPixelsSeen / browserWindowHeight ),



		//set foldsAvailable equal to the number of below-the-folds available (including the top-of-page fold)

		foldsAvailable = Math.floor( documentHeight / browserWindowHeight ),



		cookieValue = '';



		//if the tp (totalPixels) cookie isn't set yet OR if we have a pageName change OR if a reload has taken place OR if ppvChange is true AND the page has dynamically changed its size

		if(!window.cookieRead("s_tp") || decodeURIComponent(window.cookieRead("s_ppv").split(",")[0]) !== window.ppvID || window.p_fo(window.ppvID) || (window.ppvChange == true && (window.cookieRead("s_tp") && documentHeight != window.cookieRead("s_tp"))))

		{

			//When we have a new page (or reload), set the initial pixels seen

			if(decodeURIComponent(window.cookieRead("s_ppv").split(",")[0]) !== window.ppvID || window.p_fo(window.ppvID + "1")) window.cookieWrite("s_ips", totalPixelsSeen);



			//if we're still on the same page, then the page has resized (or reloaded)

			if(window.cookieRead("s_tp") && decodeURIComponent(window.cookieRead("s_ppv").split(",")[0]) === window.ppvID)

			{

				//recalculate the initialPercentViewed and highestPercentViewed (Based off most recent screen height)

				var oldHeight = window.cookieRead("s_tp"),

					currentCookie = window.cookieRead("s_ppv"),

					currentCookieArray = currentCookie.indexOf(",") > -1 ? currentCookie.split(",") : [],

					currentPage = currentCookieArray[0] ? currentCookieArray[0] : '',

					currentHighestPixelsSeen = currentCookieArray[3] ? currentCookieArray[3] : '',

					currentInitialPixelsSeen = window.cookieRead("s_ips"),

					currentHighestPercentViewed = Math.round(currentHighestPixelsSeen / documentHeight * 100),

					currentInitialPercentViewed = Math.round(currentInitialPixelsSeen / documentHeight * 100);



				cookieValue = currentPage + "," + currentHighestPercentViewed + "," + currentInitialPercentViewed + "," + currentHighestPixelsSeen + "," + foldsSeen;

			}



			//rewrite the totalPixels cookie equal to the documentHeight

			window.cookieWrite("s_tp", documentHeight);



		}

		//if the totalPixels cookie is already set, we're on the same page as before, and the page hasn't changed its size, set cookieValue equal to the "s_ppv" cookie

		else cookieValue = window.cookieRead("s_ppv");



		//setup cookieArray equal to what's in cookieValue

		var cookieArray = (cookieValue && cookieValue.indexOf(",") > -1) ? cookieValue.split(",", 6) : [],



			//set ppvID equal to window.ppvID if it didn't already exist in the cookieValue

			ppvID = cookieArray.length > 0 ? cookieArray[0] : encodeURIComponent(window.ppvID),



			//set highestPercentViewed equal to percentPixelsViewed if it didn't already exist in the cookieValue

			highestPercentViewed = cookieArray.length > 1 ? parseInt(cookieArray[1]) : percentPixelsViewed,



			//set initialPercentViewed equal to the current value of percentPixelsViewed if initialPercentViewed hasn't been determined yet (from the cookieValue)

			initialPercentViewed = cookieArray.length > 2 ? parseInt(cookieArray[2]) : percentPixelsViewed,



			//set highestTotalPixelsSeen equal to totalPixelsSeen if it didn't already exist in the cookieValue 

			highestTotalPixelsSeen = cookieArray.length > 3 ? parseInt(cookieArray[3]) : totalPixelsSeen,



			//set highestFoldsSeen equal to foldsSeen if it didn't already exist in the cookieValue 

			highestFoldsSeen = cookieArray.length > 4 ? parseInt(cookieArray[4]) : foldsSeen,



			//set highestFoldsSeen equal to foldsSeen if it didn't already exist in the cookieValue 

			highestFoldsAvailable = cookieArray.length > 5 ? parseInt(cookieArray[5]) : foldsAvailable;



		//if we have a percentPixelsViewed value, set cookieValue equal to: 

		//1. the ppvID (pageName), 

		//2. The highest percent of pixels viewed so far on that page, 

		//3. The initial percent of pixels viewed on the page, and 

		//4. the highest number of pixels scrolled down to on that page

		//5. the highest number of "folds" scrolled down to on the page

		//6. the highest number of folds available to scroll down to

		if(percentPixelsViewed > 0)

			cookieValue = ppvID + "," + 

			(percentPixelsViewed > highestPercentViewed ? percentPixelsViewed : highestPercentViewed) + "," +

			initialPercentViewed + "," +

			(totalPixelsSeen > highestTotalPixelsSeen ? totalPixelsSeen : highestTotalPixelsSeen) + "," +

			(foldsSeen > highestFoldsSeen ? foldsSeen : highestFoldsSeen) + "," +

			(foldsAvailable > highestFoldsAvailable ? foldsAvailable : highestFoldsAvailable);

		//write the s_ppv cookie (to be extracted on the next call)

		window.cookieWrite("s_ppv", cookieValue);

	};





	//set cookieValue equal to the s_ppv cookie

	var cookieValue = window.cookieRead("s_ppv"),



		//set cookieArray equal to the items in cookieValue

		cookieArray = cookieValue.indexOf(",") > -1 ? cookieValue.split(",") : [],



		//set pid equal to window.pageName OR the URL by default	

		pid = pid ? pid : window.digitalData.page.pageName ? window.digitalData.page.pageName : document.location.href;



	//decode the first item in cookieArray (usually pageName)

	cookieArray[0] = decodeURIComponent(cookieArray[0]);



	//set window.ppvChange to true by default (useful for measuring pages that change size)

	if(typeof change === "undefined" || change == true) window.ppvChange = true;

	else window.ppvChange = false;



	//if ppvID hasn't been set yet or if it's not equal to the pid argument's value (meaning we might have a new pageName)

	if(!window.ppvID || window.ppvID !== pid)

	{

		//set ppvID equal to the pid argument value

		window.ppvID = pid;



		//blank out the s_ppv cookie

		window.cookieWrite("s_ppv", "");



		//run the handlePPVevents plugin for the first time...

		handlePPVevents();

	}



	//if we're running this for the first time and we can addEventListener(s)

	if(window.p_fo("s_gppvLoad") && window.addEventListener)

	{

		//run handlePPVEvents on load, click, scroll, and resize events

		window.addEventListener("load", handlePPVevents, false);

		window.addEventListener("click", handlePPVevents, false);

		window.addEventListener("scroll", handlePPVevents, false);

	}



	//set the return variables

	return {

		ppvPreviousPage : cookieArray[0] ? cookieArray[0] : '',

		ppvHighestPercentViewed : cookieArray[1] ? cookieArray[1] : '',

		ppvInitialPercentViewed : cookieArray[2] ? cookieArray[2] : '',

		ppvHighestPixelsSeen : cookieArray[3] ? cookieArray[3] : '',

		ppvFoldsSeen : cookieArray[4] ? cookieArray[4] : '',

		ppvFoldsAvailable : cookieArray[5] ? cookieArray[5] : ''

	}

}



/********* calling plugin and add elements to data layer**********/

            widgetsUUID: widget,

            pageType: "HOME",

          },

        });

        clearInterval(intervalID);

      }

    }, 500);

  }

function checkForDigitalData(callback){

    var interval = setInterval(function(e){

        var theElement = window.digitalData;

        if(theElement.length === 0 || theElement === null) return;

        callback();

        clearInterval(interval);

    }, 400);

}



function modifyDigitalData(data) {

    checkForDigitalData(function(){

        var digitalData = window.digitalData;

        digitalData.login = data.login;

        digitalData.page.loginStatus = data.page.loginStatus;

    });

}



function checkIfStoredAnalytics() {

    var localStorageAnalytics = localStorage.getItem('analyticsInfo');

    if (localStorageAnalytics) {

        modifyDigitalData(JSON.parse(localStorageAnalytics));

    }

}

    checkIfStoredAnalytics();

}

const appendTemplate = (id, selector) => {

  const container = document.createElement("div");

  container.id = "flb-carousel-exp-" + id;

  container.innerHTML = getTemplate(id);



  const parent = document.querySelector(selector);



  if (!parent) {

    return false;

  }



  parent.appendChild(container);

  return true;

};



const addCarouselScript = () => {

  const head = document.querySelector("head");

  const previousScript = document.querySelector('script[src="' + jsCar + '"]');

  if (head && !previousScript) {

    const carrScript = document.createElement("script");

    document.querySelector("head").appendChild(carrScript);

    carrScript.src = jsCar;

  }

};



const initCarousel = (id, sku, key, widget, name, options) => {

  const carousel = document.querySelector(`#${id}`);

  if (carousel) {

    const intervalID = setInterval(() => {

      if (carousel.init) {

        carousel.init({

          title: "Productos más populares",

          tag: `Recs!Home!CO_Tienda!Rec_${key}!x!${name}`,

          dataWrapper: `C-Home_Tienda-REC${key}-${name}`,

          productPageSku: sku,

          ...options,

          inHouseConfig: {

            widgetsUUID: widget,

            pageType: "HOME",

            metadata: {

              site: "tienda", userId: digitalData.login.rutHash

            }

          },

        });

        clearInterval(intervalID);

      }

    }, 500);

  }

};



(() => {

  addCarouselScript();

  for (const key in widgets) {

    const { widget, selector, name, options } = widgets[key];

    const id = `home-tienda-rec${key}`;

    const parentExists = appendTemplate(id, selector);



    if (parentExists) {

      initCarousel(id, "home", key, widget, name, options);

    }

  }

})();



});</script>

/**

 * 

 * @param {String} cname Cookie Name

 * @param {String} cvalue Cookie Value

 * @param {Number} exdays Expiration days

 */

function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {

    var d = new Date();

    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));

    var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();

    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/;domain=.falabella.com.pe";

}



/**

 * 

 * @param {Element} element anchor element

 * @returns {Boolean} true if out of domain

 */

function isOutOfDomain(element) {

    if (element && element.tagName === 'A') {

        var url = element.href;

        url = url.indexOf('?') != -1 ? url.substring(0, url.indexOf('?')) : url;

        if (/falabella.com/.test(url)) {

            return false;

        } else if (/mi-cuenta\/giftcards/.test(url)) {

            return true;

        }

        return true;

    }

    return false;

}



var storageName = 'hometag',

    storageTLM = 'topLevelMenuCoords';



var ui = {

    isSLP: function() {

        return true;

    },

    str: function str() {

        return 'T|x|x|x|x|x|x|x|x';



    },

    approvedTrackClick: function approvedTrackClick(menulink) {

        var isMenuLink = false;

        if (/(ThirdLevelItems|SecondLevelItems|ToggleThirdCategories|thirdLevelMenu)/.test(menulink.className) || menulink && menulink.parentElement && /secondLevelMenu__/.test(menulink.parentElement.className) || menulink.closest('[class*="thirdLevelMenu__mobile"]')) {

            isMenuLink = true;

        }

        if (!isMenuLink)

            return;

        var finalCondition = false;

        finalCondition = isMenuLink;

        return finalCondition;

    },

    firstLevelDescription: function() {

        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;

        if (ui.isSLP()) {

            var menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="firstLevelMenu__"] li');

            menuItemsArr = [].slice.apply(menuItems);

            var a = menuItemsArr.find(function(element, i) {

                if (/active/.test(element.className)) {

                    return element;

                }

            });

            return windowW ? document.querySelector('[class*="firstLevelMenu__title--active"]').textContent.trim() : a.textContent.trim();

        } else {

            return windowW ? document.querySelector("#mobile-item-".concat(ui.firstLevelPosition())).textContent.trim() : document.querySelector("#item-".concat(ui.firstLevelPosition())).textContent.trim();

        }

    },

    firstLevelPosition: function() {

        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024,

            index, menuItems;

        if (ui.isSLP()) {

            if (windowW) {

                index = false;

                menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="firstLevelMenu__title"]');

                menuItemsArr = [].slice.apply(menuItems);

                menuItemsArr.map(function(element, i) {

                    if (/--active/.test(element.className)) {

                        index = i;

                    }

                });

                return index;

            } else {

                index = false;

                menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="firstLevelMenu__"] li');

                menuItemsArr = [].slice.apply(menuItems);

                menuItemsArr.map(function(element, i) {

                    if (/active/.test(element.className)) {

                        index = i;

                    }

                });

                return index;

            }

        } else {

            index = false;

            var section = window.screen.width < 1024 ? document.querySelectorAll("section[class*='menuSection'] section") : document.querySelectorAll("section[class*='menuSection'] > div > section");

            section = Array.from(section);

            section.map(function(element, i) {

                if (/display/.test(element.className)) {

                    index = i;

                }

            });



            return index;

        }

    },

    secondLevelDescription: function(theParent) {

        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;



        if (ui.isSLP()) {

            if (windowW) {

                return (theParent.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu"]') || theParent.closest('ul[class=""]').querySelector('[class*="secondLevelMenu"]')).querySelector('a').textContent.trim();

            } else {

                return theParent.querySelector('[class*="secondLevelMenu__title"]').textContent.trim();

            }



        } else {

            if (windowW) {

                return theParent.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_detailsElementsSmallDevice"]') ? theParent.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_detailsElementsSmallDevice"]').querySelector('a,p').textContent.trim() : theParent.closest('[class*=ThirdLevelItems_activeMobileThirdLevel]').previousSibling.querySelector('a,p').textContent.trim()

            } else {

                return theParent.querySelector('[class*="SecondLevelItems_submenuTitle"]').textContent.trim();



            }

        }

    },

    order: function order(el, type) {

        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024,

            thirdLevelContainer, thirdLevelLinkArr, clickedThirdLevel;

        var order = false;

        var menuLink = el;



        var columnOrder = function() {

            return windowW ? menuLink.closest("nav").querySelectorAll('[class*="firstLevelMenu"]') : menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenuContainer"]').querySelectorAll('[class*="secondLevelMenu__dekstop"]');

        };

        columnOrder = [].slice.apply(columnOrder());



        if (windowW && type === "column") {



            var newMenuLink = menuLink.closest("ul:not([class])");

            var newMenuLinkArr = [].slice.apply(newMenuLink.querySelectorAll('[class*="secondLevelMenu"]'));

            return (newMenuLinkArr.indexOf(menuLink.closest('ul[class=""]').querySelector('[class*="secondLevelMenu"]')) + 1);



        }

        //desktop

        if (!windowW && type === "column") {

            return (columnOrder.indexOf(menuLink.closest('ul[class*="secondLevelMenu"]')) + 1);

        }



        //mobile

        if (windowW && type === "row") {

            if (menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__title"]')) {

                return 0;

            } else {

                thirdLevelContainer = menuLink.closest('[class*="thirdLevelMenu__mobile"]');

                thirdLevelLinkArr = [].slice.apply(thirdLevelContainer.querySelectorAll('li'));

                clickedThirdLevel = menuLink.closest('li');

                return thirdLevelLinkArr.indexOf(clickedThirdLevel) + 1;



            }

        }



        if (!windowW && type === "row") {



            if (menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__title"]')) {

                return 0;

            } else {

                thirdLevelContainer = menuLink.closest('ul[class*="thirdLevelMenu"]');

                thirdLevelLinkArr = [].slice.apply(thirdLevelContainer.querySelectorAll('li'));

                clickedThirdLevel = menuLink.closest('li');

                return thirdLevelLinkArr.indexOf(clickedThirdLevel) + 1;



            }

        }

        var filterColum = function() {

            if (ui.isSLP()) {

                if (windowW) {

                    var a = columnOrder.find(function(el) {

                        if (el.querySelector('[class*="secondLevelMenu__title--active"]')) {

                            return el.querySelector('[class*="secondLevelMenu__title--active"]');

                        }

                    });

                    return [].slice.apply(a.querySelectorAll('[class*="secondLevelMenu__mobile"]'));

                } else {

                    return columnOrder;

                }

            } else {

                return columnOrder;

            }

        };

        filterColum().map(function(el, i) {

            var rgx = el.textContent;



            var title = function() {

                if (ui.isSLP()) {

                    return el.innerText.split("\n", 1)[0];

                } else {

                    return el.textContent.substr(0, secondLevelDescription.length);

                }

            };



            var theParent = function() {

                if (windowW) {

                    return linkTo;

                } else {

                    if (menuLink.className.indexOf("thirdLevelMenu--link") > -1 || menuLink.className.indexOf("ThirdLevelItems_submenuElementLi") > -1) {

                        return ui.isSLP() ? menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement : menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement

                    } else {

                        return menuLink.parentElement.parentElement;

                    }

                }

            };

            var secondLevelDescription = ui.secondLevelDescription(theParent());



            if (title() === secondLevelDescription) {



                if (rgx.indexOf(menuLink.textContent.trim()) > -1) {

                    var indexColumn = i;

                    var thisSlpTitle = ui.isSLP() ? /__title/.test(menuLink.className) : /_submenuTitle/.test(menuLink.className);

                    if (thisSlpTitle) {

                        if (menuLink.textContent === el.querySelector('[class*="_submenuTitle"]').textContent) {

                            switch (type) {

                                case "column":

                                    order = indexColumn;

                                    break;

                                case "row":

                                    order = /<\/a>/.test(menuLink.outerHTML) ? indexColumn = 0 : indexColumn + 1;

                                    break;

                                default:

                                    break;

                            }

                        }

                    } else {

                        var isSLPListElement = ui.isSLP() ? el.querySelectorAll('li') : el.querySelectorAll("[class*=ThirdLevelItems_listElements]");

                        // var thirdLink = windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__mobile"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=thirdLevelMenu') : isSLPListElement;

                        var thirdLink = function() {

                            if (ui.isSLP()) {

                                return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__mobile"] [class*="secondLevelMenu__content"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=thirdLevelMenu') : isSLPListElement;

                            } else {

                                // return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_displaySubMenuMobile"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=ThirdLevelItems_activeMobileThirdLevel] li') : isSLPListElement;

                                return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="activeMobileThirdLevel"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=ThirdLevelItems]') : isSLPListElement;

                            }

                        };

                        thirdLink = [].slice.apply(thirdLink());

                        thirdLink.map(function(el, i) {

                            if (el.textContent.trim() === menuLink.textContent.trim()) {

                                switch (type) {

                                    case "column":

                                        order = indexColumn;

                                        break;

                                    case "row":

                                        order = ui.isSLP() ? i - 1 : i + 1;

                                        break;

                                    default:

                                        break;

                                }

                            }

                        });

                    }

                }

            }

        });

        return order;

    }

};

            firstLevelPosition = ui.firstLevelPosition() + 1;

  <script>_satellite["_runScript16"](function(event, target, Promise) {

/**

 * prop63

 * 

 * EXP-115

 */



var storageName = "topMenuProp";



/**

 * 

 * @param {String} cname Cookie Name

 * @param {String} cvalue Cookie Value

 * @param {Number} exdays Expiration days

 */

function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {

    var d = new Date();

    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));

    var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();

    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/;domain=.falabella.com.pe";

}

/**

 * 

 * @param {Element} element 

 */

function findAnchor(element) {

    return element.tagName != 'A' ?

        element.closest('a') ? element.closest('a') : element.querySelector('a') :

        element;

}

/**

 * 

 * @param {Element} element anchor element

 * @returns {Boolean} true if out of domain

 */

function isOutOfDomain(element) {

    if (element.tagName === 'A') {

        var url = element.href;

        url = url.indexOf('?') != -1 ? url.substring(0, url.indexOf('?')) : url;

        if (/falabella.com/.test(url)) {

            return false;

        } else if (/mi-cuenta\/giftcards/.test(url)) {

            return true;

        }

        return true;

    }

    return false;

}

/**

 * 

 * @param {Element} element 

 * @returns {String} with Store Name

 */

function getStoreNameByElement(element) {

    if (element.tagName === 'A') {

        var url = element.href;

        //remove parameters

        url = url.indexOf('?') != -1 ? url.substring(0, url.indexOf('?')) : url;

        return 'Store ' + (url.includes('sodimac') ? 'Sodimac' :

            url.includes('linio') ? 'Linio' :

            url.includes('tottus') ? 'Tottus' :

            url.includes('tienda') && url.includes('falabella-') ? 'Falabella' :

            'none');

    }

    return '';

}

/**

 * 

 * @param {Event} e Event

 * @param {String} level level of event (N1, N2, etc.)

 * @param {Boolean} hardAnchor boolean to hard clicked anchor

 * @param {Boolean} isStore

 * @param {String} text string to send on tag

 */

function handleEvent(e, level, hardAnchor, isStore, text) {



    var element = findAnchor(e.target);

    if (hardAnchor && !['A', 'B'].includes(e.target.tagName)) {

        if (!(text === 'UA' && element.innerText.toUpperCase() == 'MIS CMR PUNTOS' && ['P', 'DIV'].includes(e.target.tagName))) {

            return;

        }

    }



    var obj = {

        l: level,

        n: isStore ? getStoreNameByElement(element) : text && text !== 'UA' ? text : element.innerText,

        ood: isOutOfDomain(element || e)

    };



    setCookie(storageName, '', -1);

    setCookie(storageName, btoa(JSON.stringify(obj)), 1);







    if (obj.ood && _satellite) {

        _satellite.track('OOD_CALL');

    }



}
